- [Einen Nachrichten-Batch abbrechen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.
- [Amazon Bedrock API](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/claude-on-amazon-bedrock): Anthropics Claude-Modelle sind jetzt über Amazon Bedrock allgemein verfügbar.
- [Vertex AI API](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/claude-on-vertex-ai): Die Claude-Modelle von Anthropic sind jetzt über [Vertex AI](https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai) allgemein verfügbar.
- [Client SDKs](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/client-sdks): Wir stellen Bibliotheken in Python und TypeScript zur Verfügung, die die Arbeit mit der Anthropic API erleichtern.
- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Erstellen eines Nachrichten-Batches](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.
- [Fehler](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/errors)
- [Hilfe erhalten](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/getting-help): Wir haben versucht, in dieser Dokumentation die Antworten auf die häufigsten Fragen bereitzustellen. Wenn Sie jedoch weitere technische Unterstützung bei der Verwendung von Claude, der Anthropic API oder einem unserer Produkte benötigen, können Sie sich an unser Support-Team unter [support.anthropic.com](https://support.anthropic.com) wenden.
- [Erste Schritte](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/getting-started)
- [IP-Adressen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/ip-addresses): Anthropic-Dienste sind unter einem festen Bereich von IP-Adressen erreichbar. Sie können diese zu Ihrer Firewall hinzufügen, um den minimalen Oberflächenbereich für ausgehenden Datenverkehr beim Zugriff auf die Anthropic API und Konsole zu öffnen. Diese Bereiche werden sich nicht ohne Vorankündigung ändern.
- [Nachrichtenstapel auflisten](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/listing-message-batches): List all Message Batches within a Workspace. Most recently created batches are returned first.
- [Create a Message](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/messages): Send a structured list of input messages with text and/or image content, and the model will generate the next message in the conversation.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.
- [Nachrichtenbatch-Beispiele](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/messages-batch-examples): Beispiele für die Verwendung der Message Batches API
- [Nachrichten-Token zählen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/messages-count-tokens): Count the number of tokens in a Message.

The Token Count API can be used to count the number of tokens in a Message, including tools, images, and documents, without creating it.
- [Nachrichten-Beispiele](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/messages-examples): Anfrage- und Antwortbeispiele für die Messages API
- [Streaming von Nachrichten](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/messages-streaming)
- [Migration von Text Completions](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages): Migration von Text Completions zu Messages
- [Get a Model](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/models): Get a specific model.

The Models API response can be used to determine information about a specific model or resolve a model alias to a model ID.
- [List Models](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/models-list): List available models.

The Models API response can be used to determine which models are available for use in the API. More recently released models are listed first.
- [Prompt-Validierung](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/prompt-validation): Mit Text Completions
- [Nutzungsbeschränkungen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/rate-limits): Um Missbrauch zu verhindern und die Kapazität unserer API zu verwalten, haben wir Beschränkungen für die Nutzung der Claude API durch Organisationen eingeführt.
- [Abrufen von Nachrichten-Batch-Ergebnissen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Nachrichtenstapel abrufen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [Versionen](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/api/versioning): Bei API-Anfragen müssen Sie einen `anthropic-version` Request-Header senden. Zum Beispiel `anthropic-version: 2023-06-01`. Wenn Sie unsere [Client-Bibliotheken](/de/api/client-libraries) verwenden, wird dies automatisch für Sie erledigt.

In diesem Leitfaden besprechen wir, wie Claude zur Moderation von Inhalten in Ihrer digitalen Anwendung eingesetzt werden kann.

- [Juristische Zusammenfassung](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/docs/about-claude/use-case-guides/legal-summarization): Diese Anleitung zeigt, wie man Claudes fortschrittliche Verarbeitungsfähigkeiten für natürliche Sprache nutzen kann, um juristische Dokumente effizient zusammenzufassen, wichtige Informationen zu extrahieren und die juristische Recherche zu beschleunigen. Mit Claude können Sie die Überprüfung von Verträgen, die Prozessvorbereitung und regulatorische Arbeiten optimieren, Zeit sparen und die Genauigkeit Ihrer rechtlichen Prozesse sicherstellen.

- [Einführung in Claude](https://docs.anthropic.com/de/docs/intro-to-claude): Claude ist eine Familie von [hochleistungsfähigen und intelligenten KI-Modellen](/de/docs/about-claude/models), die von Anthropic entwickelt wurde. Während Claude leistungsstark und erweiterbar ist, ist es auch die vertrauenswürdigste und zuverlässigste verfügbare KI. Sie folgt kritischen Protokollen, macht weniger Fehler und ist resistent gegen Jailbreaks - was [Unternehmenskunden](https://www.anthropic.com/customers) ermöglicht, die sichersten KI-gestützten Anwendungen im großen Maßstab zu entwickeln.

- [Cancel a Message Batch](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Create a Message Batch](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Retrieve Message Batch Results](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Retrieve a Message Batch](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [Cancelar un Lote de Mensajes](https://docs.anthropic.com/es/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/es/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Crear un Lote de Mensajes](https://docs.anthropic.com/es/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Obtener Resultados del Lote de Mensajes](https://docs.anthropic.com/es/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Recuperar un Lote de Mensajes](https://docs.anthropic.com/es/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [Annuler un Lot de Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/fr/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Créer un Lot de Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/fr/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Récupérer les Résultats du Lot de Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/fr/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Récupérer un Lot de Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/fr/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

Bien que Claude soit puissant et extensible, c'est aussi l'IA la plus fiable et la plus sûre disponible. Il suit des protocoles critiques, fait moins d'erreurs et résiste aux tentatives de contournement—permettant aux [clients entreprises](https://www.anthropic.com/customers) de créer les applications alimentées par l'IA les plus sûres à grande échelle.

- [Membatalkan Batch Pesan](https://docs.anthropic.com/id/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/id/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Membuat Batch Pesan](https://docs.anthropic.com/id/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.

- [Mengambil Hasil Batch Pesan](https://docs.anthropic.com/id/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Mengambil Batch Pesan](https://docs.anthropic.com/id/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [Annulla un Lotto di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.
- [API di Amazon Bedrock](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/claude-on-amazon-bedrock): I modelli Claude di Anthropic sono ora generalmente disponibili attraverso Amazon Bedrock.
- [API di Vertex AI](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/claude-on-vertex-ai): I modelli Claude di Anthropic sono ora generalmente disponibili attraverso [Vertex AI](https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai).
- [SDK Client](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/client-sdks): Forniamo librerie in Python e TypeScript che rendono più semplice lavorare con l'API di Anthropic.
- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Crea un Batch di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.
- [Errori](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/errors)
- [Ottenere aiuto](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/getting-help): Abbiamo cercato di fornire le risposte alle domande più comuni in questa documentazione. Tuttavia, se hai bisogno di ulteriore supporto tecnico per l'utilizzo di Claude, l'API di Anthropic o qualsiasi dei nostri prodotti, puoi contattare il nostro team di supporto su [support.anthropic.com](https://support.anthropic.com).

Puoi aggiungere questi al tuo firewall per aprire la minima superficie necessaria per il traffico in uscita quando accedi all'API e alla Console Anthropic. Questi intervalli non cambieranno senza preavviso.
- [Elenco dei Lotti di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/listing-message-batches): List all Message Batches within a Workspace. Most recently created batches are returned first.
- [Create a Message](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/messages): Send a structured list of input messages with text and/or image content, and the model will generate the next message in the conversation.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.
- [Esempi di Batch di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/messages-batch-examples): Esempi di utilizzo per l'API dei Batch di Messaggi
- [Conteggio dei token dei messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/messages-count-tokens): Count the number of tokens in a Message.

The Token Count API can be used to count the number of tokens in a Message, including tools, images, and documents, without creating it.

- [Messaggi in Streaming](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/messages-streaming)

- [Get a Model](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/models): Get a specific model.

The Models API response can be used to determine information about a specific model or resolve a model alias to a model ID.
- [List Models](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/models-list): List available models.

The Models API response can be used to determine which models are available for use in the API. More recently released models are listed first.
- [Validazione del prompt](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/prompt-validation): Con Text Completions
- [Limiti di utilizzo](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/rate-limits): Per mitigare l'uso improprio e gestire la capacità della nostra API, abbiamo implementato limiti su quanto un'organizzazione può utilizzare l'API di Claude.
- [Recupera i Risultati del Batch di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Recupera un Lotto di Messaggi](https://docs.anthropic.com/it/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [メッセージバッチのキャンセル](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.
- [Amazon Bedrock API](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/claude-on-amazon-bedrock): AnthropicのClaudeモデルがAmazon Bedrockで一般提供されるようになりました。
- [Vertex AI API](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/claude-on-vertex-ai): AnthropicのClaudeモデルは現在[Vertex AI](https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai)で一般提供されています。
- [クライアントSDK](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/client-sdks): AnthropicのAPIをより簡単に使用できるようにするPythonとTypeScriptのライブラリを提供しています。
- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [メッセージバッチの作成](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Create a Message](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/messages): Send a structured list of input messages with text and/or image content, and the model will generate the next message in the conversation.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.

- [メッセージバッチ結果の取得](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [メッセージバッチの取得](https://docs.anthropic.com/ja/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [메시지 배치 취소](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.
- [Amazon Bedrock API](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/claude-on-amazon-bedrock): Anthropic의 Claude 모델이 이제 Amazon Bedrock을 통해 일반적으로 사용 가능합니다.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [메시지 배치 생성](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Create a Message](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/messages): Send a structured list of input messages with text and/or image content, and the model will generate the next message in the conversation.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.

- [메시지 배치 결과 검색](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [메시지 배치 검색](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [버전](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/api/versioning): API 요청을 할 때는 `anthropic-version` 요청 헤더를 보내야 합니다. 예를 들어, `anthropic-version: 2023-06-01`과 같습니다. [클라이언트 라이브러리](/ko/api/client-libraries)를 사용하는 경우 이는 자동으로 처리됩니다.

- [모델](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/models): Claude는 Anthropic이 개발한 최첨단 대규모 언어 모델군입니다. 이 가이드에서는 우리의 모델들을 소개하고 기존 모델들과의 성능을 비교합니다.
- [보안 및 규정 준수](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/security-compliance)
- [콘텐츠 관리](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/use-case-guides/content-moderation): 콘텐츠 관리는 디지털 애플리케이션에서 안전하고 존중되며 생산적인 환경을 유지하는 데 중요한 측면입니다. 이 가이드에서는 Claude를 사용하여 디지털 애플리케이션 내의 콘텐츠를 관리하는 방법을 설명합니다.
- [고객 지원 상담원](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/use-case-guides/customer-support-chat): 이 가이드는 Claude의 고급 대화 기능을 활용하여 실시간으로 고객 문의를 처리하고, 24/7 지원을 제공하며, 대기 시간을 줄이고, 정확한 응답과 긍정적인 상호작용으로 대량의 지원 요청을 관리하는 방법을 설명합니다.
- [법률 문서 요약](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/use-case-guides/legal-summarization): 이 가이드는 Claude의 고급 자연어 처리 기능을 활용하여 법률 문서를 효율적으로 요약하고, 핵심 정보를 추출하며, 법률 연구를 신속하게 처리하는 방법을 설명합니다. Claude를 사용하면 계약서 검토, 소송 준비 및 규제 업무를 간소화하여 시간을 절약하고 법적 절차의 정확성을 보장할 수 있습니다.

- [티켓 라우팅](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/about-claude/use-case-guides/ticket-routing): 이 가이드는 고객 의도, 긴급성, 우선순위, 고객 프로필 등을 기반으로 대규모 고객 지원 티켓을 분류하기 위해 Claude의 고급 자연어 이해 기능을 활용하는 방법을 설명합니다.

- [Claude 소개](https://docs.anthropic.com/ko/docs/intro-to-claude): Claude는 Anthropic이 개발한 [고성능 및 지능형 AI 모델](/ko/docs/about-claude/models) 제품군입니다. Claude는 강력하고 확장 가능하면서도 가장 신뢰할 수 있고 안정적인 AI입니다. 중요한 프로토콜을 따르고, 실수가 적으며, 해킹에 강한 내성을 가지고 있어 [기업 고객](https://www.anthropic.com/customers)이 대규모로 가장 안전한 AI 기반 애플리케이션을 구축할 수 있습니다.

- [Cancelar um Lote de Mensagens](https://docs.anthropic.com/pt/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/pt/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Criar um Lote de Mensagens](https://docs.anthropic.com/pt/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Recuperar Resultados do Lote de Mensagens](https://docs.anthropic.com/pt/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.

- [Отмена пакета сообщений](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [Создание пакета сообщений](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [Получение результатов пакета сообщений](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [Получить пакет сообщений](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [Введение в Claude](https://docs.anthropic.com/ru/docs/intro-to-claude): Claude - это семейство [высокопроизводительных и интеллектуальных ИИ-моделей](/ru/docs/about-claude/models), созданных компанией Anthropic. Хотя Claude является мощным и расширяемым, это также самый надежный и достоверный ИИ из доступных. Он следует критически важным протоколам, делает меньше ошибок и устойчив к взломам, позволяя [корпоративным клиентам](https://www.anthropic.com/customers) создавать самые безопасные ИИ-приложения в масштабе.

- [取消消息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.
- [Amazon Bedrock API](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/claude-on-amazon-bedrock): Anthropic的Claude模型现已通过Amazon Bedrock全面上市。
- [Vertex AI API](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/claude-on-vertex-ai): Anthropic的Claude模型现已通过[Vertex AI](https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai)全面上线。
- [客户端 SDK](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/client-sdks): 我们提供 Python 和 TypeScript 库，使得使用 Anthropic API 变得更加容易。
- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [创建消息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [IP地址](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/ip-addresses): Anthropic服务使用固定范围的IP地址。您可以将这些地址添加到防火墙中，以便在访问Anthropic API和控制台时开放最小的出口流量。这些范围在未经通知的情况下不会改变。
- [列出消息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/listing-message-batches): List all Message Batches within a Workspace. Most recently created batches are returned first.
- [Create a Message](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/messages): Send a structured list of input messages with text and/or image content, and the model will generate the next message in the conversation.

The Messages API can be used for either single queries or stateless multi-turn conversations.
- [消息批次示例](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/messages-batch-examples): 消息批次 API 的使用示例
- [计算消息令牌数](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/messages-count-tokens): Count the number of tokens in a Message.

The Token Count API can be used to count the number of tokens in a Message, including tools, images, and documents, without creating it.
- [消息示例](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/messages-examples): 消息 API 的请求和响应示例
- [流式消息](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/messages-streaming)
- [从文本补全迁移](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages): 从文本补全迁移到消息
- [Get a Model](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/models): Get a specific model.

The Models API response can be used to determine information about a specific model or resolve a model alias to a model ID.
- [List Models](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/models-list): List available models.

The Models API response can be used to determine which models are available for use in the API. More recently released models are listed first.
- [提示验证](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/prompt-validation): 使用文本补全
- [速率限制](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/rate-limits): 为了减少滥用并管理我们API的容量，我们对组织使用Claude API的数量实施了限制。
- [获取消息批次结果](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.
- [检索消息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-CN/api/retrieving-message-batches): This endpoint is idempotent and can be used to poll for Message Batch completion. To access the results of a Message Batch, make a request to the `results_url` field in the response.

- [取消訊息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/api/canceling-message-batches): Batches may be canceled any time before processing ends. Once cancellation is initiated, the batch enters a `canceling` state, at which time the system may complete any in-progress, non-interruptible requests before finalizing cancellation.

The number of canceled requests is specified in `request_counts`. To determine which requests were canceled, check the individual results within the batch. Note that cancellation may not result in any canceled requests if they were non-interruptible.

- [Create a Text Completion](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/api/complete): [Legacy] Create a Text Completion.

The Text Completions API is a legacy API. We recommend using the [Messages API](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages) going forward.

Future models and features will not be compatible with Text Completions. See our [migration guide](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/migrating-from-text-completions-to-messages) for guidance in migrating from Text Completions to Messages.
- [建立訊息批次](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/api/creating-message-batches): Send a batch of Message creation requests.

The Message Batches API can be used to process multiple Messages API requests at once. Once a Message Batch is created, it begins processing immediately. Batches can take up to 24 hours to complete.

- [檢索訊息批次結果](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/api/retrieving-message-batch-results): Streams the results of a Message Batch as a `.jsonl` file.

Each line in the file is a JSON object containing the result of a single request in the Message Batch. Results are not guaranteed to be in the same order as requests. Use the `custom_id` field to match results to requests.

- [倫理困境導航器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/ethical-dilemma-navigator): 幫助用戶思考複雜的倫理困境並提供不同的觀點
- [Excel公式專家](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/excel-formula-expert): 根據用戶描述的計算或數據操作創建Excel公式。
- [函數生成器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/function-fabricator): 根據詳細規格創建 Python 函數。
- [未來主義時尚顧問](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/futuristic-fashion-advisor): 根據用戶的具體偏好建議前衛時尚趨勢和風格
- [精通 Git](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/git-gud): 根據使用者描述的版本控制操作生成適當的 Git 命令。
- [Google Apps 腳本編寫器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/google-apps-scripter): 根據用戶需求生成 Google Apps 腳本以完成任務。
- [評分專家](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/grading-guru): 根據用戶定義的標準和準則比較和評估文本的質量
- [文法精靈](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/grammar-genie): 將語法不正確的句子轉換為正確的英語。
- [幽默助手Hal](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/hal-the-humorous-helper): 與一位具有諷刺性格的知識豐富AI聊天。
- [成語解析器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/idiom-illuminator): 解釋常見成語和諺語的含義及來源
- [面試問題生成器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/interview-question-crafter): 生成面試問題。
- [LaTeX 圖例](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/latex-legend): 撰寫 LaTeX 文件，生成數學方程式、表格等代碼。
- [課程計劃制定工具](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/lesson-planner): 在任何學科上制定深入的課程計劃。
- [提示庫](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/library)
- [主要審核者](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/master-moderator): 評估用戶輸入是否包含潛在有害或非法內容
- [會議記錄員](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/meeting-scribe): 將會議內容提煉為簡潔的摘要，包括討論主題、重要結論和行動項目。
- [備忘錄大師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/memo-maestro): 根據關鍵要點撰寫全面的公司備忘錄
- [正念導師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/mindfulness-mentor): 引導用戶進行正念練習和減壓技巧
- [情緒色彩轉換器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/mood-colorizer): 將情緒文字描述轉換為相應的十六進制顏色代碼。
- [激勵繆思](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/motivational-muse): 根據用戶輸入提供個性化的激勵訊息和肯定語
- [新詞創造器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/neologism-creator): 根據用戶提供的概念或想法發明新詞並提供其定義。
- [觀點權衡者](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/perspectives-ponderer): 權衡使用者提供主題的利弊。
- [哲學思考](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/philosophical-musings): 進行深度哲學討論和思想實驗。
- [PII 淨化器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/pii-purifier): 自動檢測並移除文本文件中的個人身份識別資訊 (PII)。
- [多語言超能力](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/polyglot-superpowers): 將任何語言翻譯成任何語言。
- [組合詞詩人](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/portmanteau-poet): 將兩個詞組合在一起創造一個新的、有意義的組合詞。
- [產品命名專家](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/product-naming-pro): 從描述和關鍵字創建引人注目的產品名稱
- [文章修飾器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/prose-polisher): 使用進階文字編輯技巧和建議來改進和提升書面內容。
- [雙關語大師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/pun-dit): 根據任何給定主題生成巧妙的雙關語和文字遊戲。
- [Python 除錯工具](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/python-bug-buster): 檢測並修復 Python 程式碼中的錯誤。
- [評論分類器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/review-classifier): 將反饋分類為預先指定的標籤和類別。
- [來猜個謎語吧](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/riddle-me-this): 生成謎語並引導使用者找到答案
- [科幻場景模擬器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/sci-fi-scenario-simulator): 與用戶討論各種科幻場景及其相關挑戰和考慮因素。
- [二年級簡化器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/second-grade-simplifier): 讓複雜的文字變得容易讓年輕學習者理解
- [比喻大師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/simile-savant): 從基本描述生成比喻。
- [蘇格拉底式智者](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/socratic-sage): 以蘇格拉底式對話方式討論用戶給定的主題
- [試算表魔術師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/spreadsheet-sorcerer): 生成包含各種類型數據的 CSV 試算表。
- [SQL 魔法師](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/sql-sorcerer): 將日常語言轉換為 SQL 查詢。
- [說故事小幫手](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/storytelling-sidekick): 與使用者協作創作引人入勝的故事，提供情節轉折和角色發展。
- [時間旅行顧問](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/time-travel-consultant): 幫助用戶探索假設性時間旅行場景及其影響。
- [繞口令](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/tongue-twister): 創建富有挑戰性的繞口令。
- [問答遊戲生成器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/trivia-generator): 在各種主題上生成問答題目，並在需要時提供提示。
- [推文語氣偵測器](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/tweet-tone-detector): 偵測推文背後的語氣和情感。
- [VR 健身創新者](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/vr-fitness-innovator): 為虛擬實境健身遊戲集思廣益創意點子。
- [網站精靈](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/prompt-library/website-wizard): 根據用戶規格創建單頁網站。
- [API](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/release-notes/api): 追蹤 Anthropic 的 API 和開發者控制台的最新更新。
- [Claude 應用程式](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/release-notes/claude-apps): 追蹤 Anthropic 的 Claude 應用程式的最新更新。
- [概述](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/release-notes/overview): 追蹤 Anthropic 產品和服務的最新更新。
- [系統提示詞](https://docs.anthropic.com/zh-TW/release-notes/system-prompts): 查看 [Claude.ai](https://www.claude.ai) 和 Claude [iOS](http://anthropic.com/ios) 及 [Android](http://anthropic.com/android) 應用程式的核心系統提示詞更新。
